    <script type="text/javascript">
     function NotNull(x) {
                if (x == null || x == "") {
                    alert("Please enter a word to rhyme");
                    return false;
                }
                return true;
            }

            function validate() {
                return (NotNull(document.forms["Rhymer"]["Word"].value));
            }

            function validate2() {
                return (NotNull(document.forms["Rhymer2"]["Word"].value));
            }

            function runRhymer() {
                if (document.Rhymer.RhymeType.value == "EndRhymes") {
                    window.location = "/RhymingDictionary/" + document.Rhymer.Word.value + ".html"
                }
                else {
                    window.location = "/RhymingDictionary" + document.Rhymer.RhymeType.value + "/" + document.Rhymer.Word.value + ".html"
                }
            }

            function runRhymer2() {
                if (document.Rhymer2.RhymeType.value == "EndRhymes") {
                    window.location = "/RhymingDictionary/" + document.Rhymer2.Word.value + ".html"
                }
                else {
                    window.location = "/RhymingDictionary" + document.Rhymer2.RhymeType.value + "/" + document.Rhymer2.Word.value + ".html"
                }
            }
    </script>
